 Security Content c2108.2 Release Notes
=======================================

These Release Notes document security content updates from content package c2106.2 to c2108.2.

The security content updates listed below include changes to the following areas:

* [Parsers](#Parsers)

* [Models](#Models)

* [Rules](#Rules)

In the lists below, each item represents a specific parser, model, or rule that has been added, updated, or deprecated. To facilitate finding every data source where the changed content items are referenced, a content library query has been created for each changed parser, model, or rule. To view the results of each query, click on the link for the relevant content item.

Parsers
-------

* [New](#New-Parsers)

* [Updated](#Updated-Parsers)

* [Deprecated](#Deprecated-Parsers)

#### Deprecated Parsers

Models
------
* [New](#New-Models)

* [Updated](#Updated-Models)

* [Deprecated](#Deprecated-Models)

#### New Models
* [A-AC-DhU-system](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AC-DhU-system) &#8211; System accounts performing account creation activities

* [A-AE-AEtype](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AE-AEtype) &#8211; Event types per asset

* [A-AE-NTLM](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AE-NTLM) &#8211; Models the NTLM hostnames seen in the organization

* [A-AE-OHr](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AE-OHr) &#8211; Random hostnames on asset

* [A-AE-UA-src](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AE-UA-src) &#8211; All activity for assets (src)

* [A-AE-UA](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AE-UA) &#8211; All activity for assets

* [A-AE-UU](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AE-UU) &#8211; All activity by users on assets

* [A-AE-ZEtype](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AE-ZEtype) &#8211; Event types per zone

* [A-AL-DhU-count](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AL-DhU-count) &#8211; Number of users logging into assets

* [A-AL-DhUP](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AL-DhUP) &#8211; Peer groups per Host

* [A-AL-DhU](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AL-DhU) &#8211; Users per Host

* [A-AL-ZT-SERVER](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AL-ZT-SERVER) &#8211; Server zones based on number of servers

* [A-AM-DhU-system](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-AM-DhU-system) &#8211; System accounts performing account management activities

* [A-DB-AN-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DB-AN-ALERT) &#8211; Database alert names on asset

* [A-DB-OA-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DB-OA-ALERT) &#8211; Assets triggering database alerts in the organization

* [A-DB-ON-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DB-ON-ALERT) &#8211; Database alert names triggered in the organization

* [A-DB-ZA-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DB-ZA-ALERT) &#8211; Assets triggering database alerts in the zone

* [A-DB-ZN-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DB-ZN-ALERT) &#8211; Database alert names triggered in the zone

* [A-DLP-AN-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DLP-AN-ALERT) &#8211; DLP alert names on asset

* [A-DLP-AN-FREQ](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DLP-AN-FREQ) &#8211; INTERNAL: DLP alert names on asset

* [A-DLP-HN-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DLP-HN-ALERT) &#8211; DLP alert names triggered in the asset

* [A-DLP-OA-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DLP-OA-ALERT) &#8211; Assets triggering DLP alerts in the organization

* [A-DLP-ON-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DLP-ON-ALERT) &#8211; DLP alert names triggered in the organization

* [A-DLP-ZN-ALERT](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DLP-ZN-ALERT) &#8211; DLP alert names triggered in the zone

* [A-DNS-ABSum](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DNS-ABSum) &#8211; Sum of bytes of DNS queries in a sequence for asset

* [A-DNS-AQCount](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DNS-AQCount) &#8211; Count of DNS queries in a sequence for the asset

* [A-DNS-AQNXCount](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DNS-AQNXCount) &#8211; Count of DNS queries to NX domains in a sequence for the asset

* [A-DNS-OBSum](https://github.com/ExabeamLabs/Content-Doc/search?q=A-DNS-OBSum) &#8211; Sum of bytes of DNS queries in the organization
